    <a id="2434" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="2439" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2319" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="2442" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2443" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2393" class="Bound">αᵉ</a> <a id="2446" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a> <a id="2449" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2410" class="Bound">βᵉ</a><a id="2451" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2453" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2800" class="Function Operator">~ᵉ</a> <a id="2456" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="2461" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2319" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="2464" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2393" class="Bound">αᵉ</a> <a id="2467" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3445" class="Function Operator">∙hᵉ</a> <a id="2471" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="2476" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2319" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="2479" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2410" class="Bound">βᵉ</a>
  <a id="2484" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2349" class="Function">tr²-concatᵉ</a> <a id="2496" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2496" class="Bound">αᵉ</a> <a id="2499" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2499" class="Bound">βᵉ</a> <a id="2502" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2502" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="2505" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2507" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2088" class="Function">ap-concatᵉ</a> <a id="2518" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="2521" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2521" class="Bound">tᵉ</a> <a id="2524" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2526" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#837" class="Function">trᵉ</a> <a id="2530" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2319" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="2533" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2521" class="Bound">tᵉ</a> <a id="2536" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2502" class="Bound">bᵉ</a><a id="2538" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2540" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2496" class="Bound">αᵉ</a> <a id="2543" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2499" class="Bound">βᵉ</a>

#### Computing `tr²` along the inverse of an identification

    <a id="3189" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="3194" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2680" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="3197" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3167" class="Bound">αᵉ</a> <a id="3200" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3445" class="Function Operator">∙hᵉ</a> <a id="3204" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="3209" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2680" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="3212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3213" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="3218" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3167" class="Bound">αᵉ</a><a id="3220" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3222" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2800" class="Function Operator">~ᵉ</a> <a id="3225" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3017" class="Function">refl-htpyᵉ</a>

#### Computing tr³ along the unit laws for whiskering of identifications

These coherences take the form of the following commutative diagrams. Note that
there is an asymmetry between the left and right coherence laws due to the
asymmetry in the definition of concatenation of identifications.

The above coherences have simplified forms when we consider 2-loops

                <a id="11937" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11939" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3017" class="Function">refl-htpyᵉ</a><a id="11949" class="Symbol">)</a>
                <a id="11967" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11969" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4335" class="Function">left-unit-law-left-whisker-compᵉ</a> <a id="12002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12003" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="12008" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8746" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="12011" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9522" class="Bound">αᵉ</a><a id="12013" class="Symbol">))))</a>
            <a id="12030" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12032" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9990" class="Function">ap-inv-htpyᵉ</a>
              <a id="12059" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12061" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies-concatenation%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3015" class="Function">left-unit-law-left-whisker-concat-htpyᵉ</a>
                <a id="12117" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12119" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4335" class="Function">left-unit-law-left-whisker-compᵉ</a> <a id="12152" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12153" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="12158" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8746" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="12161" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9522" class="Bound">αᵉ</a><a id="12163" class="Symbol">))))</a>

              <a id="12245" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12247" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12249" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2349" class="Function">tr²-concatᵉ</a> <a id="12261" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12262" href="foundation-core.whiskering-identifications-concatenation%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2241" class="Function">right-whisker-concatᵉ</a> <a id="12284" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9522" class="Bound">αᵉ</a> <a id="12287" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a><a id="12292" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12294" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a><a id="12299" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12301" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3445" class="Function Operator">∙hᵉ</a>
                <a id="12321" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12323" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3017" class="Function">refl-htpyᵉ</a><a id="12333" class="Symbol">))</a>
              <a id="12350" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12352" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1241" class="Function">tr³ᵉ</a> <a id="12357" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8746" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="12360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12361" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="12366" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12367" href="foundation-core.whiskering-identifications-concatenation%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4356" class="Function">right-unit-law-right-whisker-concatᵉ</a> <a id="12404" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9522" class="Bound">αᵉ</a><a id="12406" class="Symbol">)))</a>
              <a id="12424" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12426" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4357" class="Function">tr²-right-whiskerᵉ</a> <a id="12445" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9522" class="Bound">αᵉ</a> <a id="12448" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a><a id="12453" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="12469" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12471" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3214" class="Function">inv-htpyᵉ</a>
                <a id="12497" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12499" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies-concatenation%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1568" class="Function">left-whisker-concat-htpyᵉ</a>
                  <a id="12543" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12545" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3017" class="Function">refl-htpyᵉ</a><a id="12555" class="Symbol">)</a>
                  <a id="12575" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12577" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4335" class="Function">left-unit-law-left-whisker-compᵉ</a> <a id="12610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12611" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#989" class="Function">tr²ᵉ</a> <a id="12616" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8746" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="12619" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9522" class="Bound">αᵉ</a><a id="12621" class="Symbol">))))</a>
              <a id="12640" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12642" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5849" class="Function">right-unit-htpyᵉ</a><a id="12658" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="12674" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12676" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7820" class="Function">tr³-right-unit-law-right-whisker-concatᵉ</a> <a id="12717" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9522" class="Bound">αᵉ</a><a id="12719" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
</pre>
#### Computing `tr³` along `commutative-left-whisker-right-whisker-concat`

This coherence naturally takes the form of a filler for a cube whose left face
is

```text
tr³ B (commutative-left-whisker-right-whisker-concat β α)
```

and whose right face is

```text
commutative-right-whisker-left-whisker-htpy (tr² B β) (tr² B α)
```

However, this cube has trivial front and back faces. Thus, we only prove a
simplified form of the coherence.

##### Non-trivial faces of the cube

<pre class="Agda"><a id="13217" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="13224" href="foundation.transport-along-higher-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13224" class="Module">_</a>

##### A simplification of the main coherence when `α` and `β` are 2-loops
